<script type="text/javascript"> 
	function addTreeParm(treeid) {
		if(treeid == 0)
			return;
		var url = window.location.href;  
		var idx = url.indexOf('tid='); 
		if(idx==-1){
			url += '&tid=' + dnaForm.matchPublicTreeIds[treeid-1];
			url += '&hpid=' + dnaForm.matchTreeHomePids[treeid-1];
		}
		else {
			url = url.substring(0, idx+4) + dnaForm.matchPublicTreeIds[treeid-1];
			url += '&hpid=' + dnaForm.matchTreeHomePids[treeid-1];
		}
		window.location.href = url;
	}
</script>

					<script type="text/javascript">
						//"No Tree" image carousel Javascript
						var subjectNoTree=new CarouselObj({
							'id':'subjectNoTree',
							'maxWorH':500,
							'timeToPause':2000,
							'autoPlay':false,
							'noWrap':true,
							'pagElms':[document.getElementById('lrg1Btn'),document.getElementById('lrg2Btn'),document.getElementById('lrg3Btn'),document.getElementById('lrg4Btn'),document.getElementById('lrg5Btn')],
							'extElmInViewFunc':function(){
								for(var a=0;a<this.pagElms.length;a++){
									this.pagElms[a].className=this.pagElms[a].className.replace('selected','');
								}
								this.pagElms[this.elmInView-1].className=this.pagElms[this.elmInView-1].className+' selected';
							},
							'extPagClickFunc':function(pagElmNum){
								if(this.timeFunc){
									clearTimeout(this.timeFunc);
									this.timeFunc=false;
								}
								this.isAnimating=false;
								this.setElmInView(pagElmNum+1);
								document.getElementById('nextBtnText').innerHTML='';
							},
							'extAnimFunc':function(){
								for(var a=0;a<this.pagElms.length;a++){
									this.pagElms[a].className=this.pagElms[a].className.replace('selected','');
								}
								if(this.elmInView>=this.listOfElms.length){
									this.pagElms[0].className=this.pagElms[0].className+' selected';
								}else{
									this.pagElms[this.elmInView].className=this.pagElms[this.elmInView].className+' selected';
								}
							},
							'extNoWrapFunc':function(){
								clearTimeout(this.timeFunc);
								this.timeFunc=false;
								this.isAnimating=false;
								document.getElementById('nextBtnText').innerHTML='Start Over';
								document.getElementById('carAutoPlay').innerHTML='Turn Auto Play On';
							}
							
						});
						function nextLrgCar(){
							subjectNoTree.animNextCar();
						}
						function prevLrgCar(){
							subjectNoTree.animPrevCar();
						}
						
						</script>

	// Get Header.
	AjaxManager.send({
		url: "http://header.ajax.ancestry.com/tabDna?loginUrl=http://dna.ancestry.com/&logoutUrl=http://dna.ancestry.com",
		success: function() {
			// Show the header.
		 	$("#HeaderRegion .headWrp .topSec, .mainNav").show();

		 	// Get Footer.
			AjaxManager.send({
				url: "http://footer.ajax.ancestry.com"
			});
		}
	});
</script>
